The bathroom and kitchen is shared. Kitchen is very small and basic-Kitchen is NOT meant for major cooking- just storing food, heating food, coffee, etc. There are 3 floors in the building. Each floor has 2 bathrooms shared among the guests on that floor. Each floor has approximately 7 rooms. If you're looking for a very basic place to stay and sleep, this space is for you. No frills. Nothing fancy. Priced for what it is. If you consider yourself a low maintenance guest, this place would be great for you. You will be responsible for your own food and toiletries. I will provide sheets, blankets, and towels. If you need anything other than what I have provided, it is up to you to purchase if you are staying for an extended period of time.
